04/2100Z: SOLAR ACTIVITY HAS BEEN AT LOW LEVELS FOR THE PAST 24 HOURS.

04/0947Z FROM REGION 2361 (N16E64). THERE ARE CURRENTLY 6 NUMBERED
SUNSPOT REGIONS ON THE DISK.
IB.  SOLAR ACTIVITY FORECAST: SOLAR ACTIVITY IS EXPECTED TO BE LOW WITH
A SLIGHT CHANCE FOR AN M-CLASS FLARE ON DAYS ONE, TWO, AND THREE (05
JUN, 06 JUN, 07 JUN).
IIA.  GEOPHYSICAL ACTIVITY SUMMARY 03/2100Z TO 04/2100Z: THE GEOMAGNETIC
FIELD HAS BEEN AT QUIET LEVELS FOR THE PAST 24 HOURS. SOLAR WIND SPEED,
AS MEASURED BY THE ACE SPACECRAFT, RANGED FROM ABOUT 250 TO 310 KM/S
DURING THE PERIOD. TOTAL IMF REACHED 6 NT AT 04/0352Z. THE MAXIMUM
SOUTHWARD COMPONENT OF BZ REACHED -3 NT AT 04/1408Z.
IIB.  GEOPHYSICAL ACTIVITY FORECAST: THE GEOMAGNETIC FIELD IS EXPECTED
TO BE AT QUIET LEVELS ON DAY ONE (05 JUN) AND QUIET TO UNSETTLED LEVELS
ON DAYS TWO AND THREE (06 JUN, 07 JUN).

  PRESTO
  w na~ale sutok 8 i`nq k zemle podo{el skorostnoj 
  solne~nyj weter, ishodq}ij ot koronalxnoj dyry.
  s 02.00 msk bylo zaregistrirowano na~alo geomagnitnogo 
  wozmu}eniq. predpolagaetsq, ~to magnitnaq burq prodlitsq 
  neskolxko sutok.
  k-indeksy po sredne{irotnym stanciqm
              00-03 03-06 06-09
  moskwa        3     3     4
  s-peterburg   /     /     5
  obzor kosmi~eskoj pogody za 05-07 i`nq 2015 goda.
  integralxnaq solne~naq aktiwnostx - umerennaq.
  na diske solnca nabl`dalosx ot semi do dewqti grupp pqten.
  naibolx{aq wspy{e~naq aktiwnostx byla zaregistrirowana 
  w nebolx{oj gruppe 2361 (N16E22, 80 mdp, w) - 7 wspy{ek 
  klassa s za troe sutok, samaq prodolvitelxnaq iz nih 
  proizo{la 6 i`nq - |to 62-minutnaq wspy{ka s1/SF w 10.12 msk.
  nizku` wspy{e~nu` aktiwnostx proqwlqli medlenno 
  razwiwaw{iesq gruppy:
  2360 (N15W04, 140 mdp, BG), 2362 (N05E27, 140 mdp, w), 
  2365 (S13E48, 90 mdp, w).
  wspy{e~naq aktiwnostx - nizkaq.
  geomagnitnoe pole.
  po dannym sredne{irotnyh stancij - o~enx spokojnoe;
  po dannym wysoko{irotnyh stancij - ot spokojnogo do o~enx 
  spokojnogo.
  radiacionnaq obstanowka na trassah pilotiruemyh kosmi~eskih
  apparatow - newozmu}ennaq.
  po dannym murmanskogo ugms srywy kw-radioswqzi 7 i`nq
  byli zaregistrirowany na trassah:
  kolxskogo poluostrowa - net;
  sewernogo i wosto~nogo naprawlenij w 02, 04 msk;
  `vnogo naprawleniq - net.
  prognoz kosmi~eskoj pogody na 8 - 9 i`nq 2015 g.
        ovidaetsq, ~to wspy{e~naq aktiwnostx budet nizkaq;
  geomagnitnoe pole: 8 i`nq - neustoj~iwoe, 9 i`nq - slabo 
  wozmu}ennoe;
